Swarm Routing Recommendations

Route Current model Verdict Alternative
conversational (M4) qwen3:8b ✅ Stays on M4 —
general/research qwen3:14b ✅ Best 14B reasoning —
code qwen2.5-coder:14b ✅ Solid, matches qwen3:14b TG speed qwen2.5-coder:7b for 6× faster TG
verify (2-pass CoT) deepseek-r1:14b ⚠️ Slowest 14B PP (608 tok/s) deepseek-r1:8b = 73 tok/s TG, much faster
heavy verify qwen3:32b ⚠️ 3 tok/s TG — use sparingly phi4 as faster 14B alternative

Key Takeaways

  • 8B models are 6× faster than 14B on this GPU (73 vs 12 tok/s TG) — worth routing shorter tasks to 8B
  • nemotron-mini is the fastest for PP throughput (4,318 tok/s) and coolest thermals — ideal for high-volume tasks
  • deepseek-r1:8b matches llama3.1:8b and qwen3:8b in TG speed (~73 tok/s) but brings native CoT — strong candidate for verify route
  • qwen3:32b is throttled by RAM spill (3 tok/s) — only use for tasks where quality justifies the wait
  • CPU is the bottleneck for 32b, not GPU — Ryzen 7 3700X memory bandwidth limits RAM-spill models
  • gemma4:e2b fills the gap between 8B and 14B — 43 tok/s TG and blazing PP (~3,400 tok/s @ pp=512), but slower than 8B models on TG; mostly running from RAM (only ~1.9GB VRAM active)
  • gemma4:26b MoE beats 14B dense models in TG (15 vs 12 tok/s) despite being 17GB — MoE only activates 4B params per token so compute is light; TTFT penalty is severe (1,430ms) due to ~9GB RAM spill; not worth routing to unless quality demands it
  • qwen3.6 (22.8GB) is the most RAM-spill-bound model tested — ~14.8GB spills to system RAM; 7 tok/s TG and ~374 tok/s PP @ pp=512; TTFT ~1,900ms; only practical for tasks where quality justifies significant latency

Full per-model reports with temperature charts follow below.

Finance Model Benchmarks — 2026-04-11

Target machine: stealth — RTX 2080 SUPER 8GB VRAM, Ryzen 7 3700X, 32GB RAM

Settings: Q8 KV cache + Flash Attention enabled (new as of this session)

Runs per test: 3 | PP sizes: 128, 512, 2048 | TG sizes: 64, 256

TG Decode Speed (tok/s)

Model Base tg64 pp128 tg256 pp128 tg64 pp2048 tg256 pp2048 GPU peak
0xroyce/plutus Llama 3.1 8B 67.7 67.3 64.4 64.6 58°C
brrndnn/mistral7b-finance Mistral 7B 66.4 65.8 62.4 62.2 66°C
jjansen/adapt-finance-llama2-7b Llama 2 7B 92.0 92.3 83.7 83.3 64°C

PP Prefill Speed (tok/s)

Model pp128 pp512 pp2048
0xroyce/plutus 3598 2270 2069
brrndnn/mistral7b-finance 1709–1823 1696–1760 1632–1633
jjansen/adapt-finance-llama2-7b 272* 2394–2974 2595–2604

*adapt-finance pp128 anomaly — likely model loading during first test; pp512+ numbers are valid.

TTFT

Model pp128 pp512 pp2048
0xroyce/plutus ~195ms ~362ms ~1050ms
brrndnn/mistral7b-finance ~106ms ~331ms ~1274ms
jjansen/adapt-finance-llama2-7b ~43ms ~193ms ~839ms

Notes

  • adapt-finance-llama2-7b is the fastest decoder at ~83–92 tok/s — significantly faster than both other finance models and most general models tested. Llama 2 7B architecture runs very efficiently on the 2080 Super.
  • Plutus is the most consistent — flat decode speed regardless of context depth, lowest temps.
  • mistral7b-finance is the slowest PP and runs hottest — least efficient of the three.
  • M4: adapt-finance-llama2-7b also installed locally (no benchmark — no nvidia-smi on Apple Silicon).
  • Full per-test reports with temp charts: ~/bench-results/ on stealth.
